Time Model Statistics

  • DB Time represents total time in user calls
  • DB CPU represents CPU time of foreground processes
  • Total CPU Time represents foreground and background processes
  • Statistics including the word "background" measure background process time, therefore do not contribute to the DB time statistic
  • Ordered by % of DB time in descending order, followed by Statistic Name

Shared Pool Advisory

  • SP: Shared Pool Est LC: Estimated Library Cache Factr: Factor
  • Note there is often a 1:Many correlation between a single logical object in the Library Cache, and the physical number of memory objects associated with it. Therefore comparing the number of Lib Cache objects (e.g. in v$librarycache), with the number of Lib Cache Memory Objects is invalid.

Undo Segment Summary

  • Min/Max TR (mins) - Min and Max Tuned Retention (minutes)
  • STO - Snapshot Too Old count, OOS - Out of Space count
  • Undo segment block stats:
  • uS - unexpired Stolen, uR - unexpired Released, uU - unexpired reUsed
  • eS - expired Stolen, eR - expired Released, eU - expired reUsed

                                             Percent of Activity
   ----------------------------------------  -------------------  ---------------

~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~


          Findings and Recommendations
          ----------------------------

Finding 1: Top SQL Statements
Impact is 1.06 active sessions, 98.85% of total activity.
---------------------------------------------------------
SQL statements consuming significant database time were found. These
statements offer a good opportunity for performance improvement.

   Recommendation 1: SQL Tuning
   Estimated benefit is 1.06 active sessions, 98.85% of total activity.
   --------------------------------------------------------------------
   Action
      Run SQL Tuning Advisor on the UPSERT statement with SQL_ID
      "03rxfh1snby0h".
      Related Object
         SQL statement with SQL_ID 03rxfh1snby0h.
         MERGE INTO PSP_LEDGER_BALANCE TGT USING (SELECT FTS.COMPANY_FK, TRUNC
         (FTS.TRANSACTION_STATE_EFF_DATE) NEWBAL_DATE, SUM ( (SELECT
         FT.FINANCIAL_TRANSACTION_AMOUNT FROM PSP_FINANCIAL_TRANSACTION FT
         WHERE FT.FINANCIAL_TRANSACTION_SEQ = FTS.FINANCIAL_TRANSACTION_FK) *
         DECODE (PR.CREDIT_DEBIT_IND, 'C', DECODE
         (LA.BALANCE_CALCULATION_RULE,'CreditAddsToBalance', 1,-1), 'D',
         DECODE (LA.BALANCE_CALCULATION_RULE,'DebitAddsToBalance', 1,-1) ) )
         AMOUNT, PR.LEDGER_ACCOUNT_FK, PO.REPORTING_TYPE FROM
         PSP_FINANCIAL_TRANS_STATE FTS, PSP_POSTING_RULE PR,
         PSP_LEDGER_ACCOUNT LA, PSP_COMPANY PC, PSP_COMPANY_OFFERING PCO,
         PSP_OFFERING PO WHERE PR.TRANSACTION_STATE_FK =
         FTS.TRANSACTION_STATE_FK AND PR.TRANSACTION_TYPE_FK =
         FTS.TRANSACTION_TYPE_FK AND LA.LEDGER_ACCOUNT_CD =
         PR.LEDGER_ACCOUNT_FK AND PC.COMPANY_SEQ=FTS.COMPANY_FK AND
         PC.COMPANY_SEQ=PCO.COMPANY_FK AND PCO.OFFERING_FK=PO.OFFERING_SEQ AND
         PO.SERVICE_CODE='DirectDeposit' AND TRUNC
         (FTS.TRANSACTION_STATE_EFF_DATE) = TRUNC(:B1 ) AND
         FTS.TRANSACTION_STATE_EFF_DATE BETWEEN :B1 - 1 AND :B1 + 1 GROUP BY
         FTS.COMPANY_FK, TRUNC (FTS.TRANSACTION_STATE_EFF_DATE),
         PR.LEDGER_ACCOUNT_FK, PO.REPORTING_TYPE) SRC ON ( TGT.COMPANY_FK =
         SRC.COMPANY_FK AND TGT.REPORTING_TYPE =SRC.REPORTING_TYPE AND
         TGT.LEDGER_ACCOUNT_FK = SRC.LEDGER_ACCOUNT_FK AND TRUNC
         (TGT.BALANCE_DATE) = TRUNC (SRC.NEWBAL_DATE)) WHEN MATCHED THEN
         UPDATE SET TGT.BALANCE_AMOUNT = TGT.BALANCE_AMOUNT + SRC.AMOUNT,
         MODIFIED_DATE = :B2 , VERSION = VERSION+1,
         MODIFIER_ID='LEDGERBALANCEBATCHJOBMERGEUPD' WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
         INSERT (TGT.LEDGER_BALANCE_SEQ, VERSION, CREATOR_ID, CREATED_DATE,
         MODIFIED_DATE, REALM_ID, BALANCE_AMOUNT, BALANCE_DATE,
         LEDGER_ACCOUNT_FK, COMPANY_FK, REPORTING_TYPE) VALUES
         (FN_FORMAT_SYSGUID (SYS_GUID ()), 1, 'LEDGERBALANCEBATCHJOBMERGEINS',
         :B2 , :B2 , -1, NVL((SELECT ILB.BALANCE_AMOUNT FROM
         PSP_LEDGER_BALANCE ILB WHERE
         ILB.LEDGER_ACCOUNT_FK=SRC.LEDGER_ACCOUNT_FK AND
         ILB.COMPANY_FK=SRC.COMPANY_FK AND TRUNC(ILB.BALANCE_DATE) = (SELECT
         TRUNC(MAX(TRUNC(OLB.BALANCE_DATE))) FROM PSP_LEDGER_BALANCE OLB WHERE
         OLB.COMPANY_FK=ILB.COMPANY_FK AND
         OLB.LEDGER_ACCOUNT_FK=ILB.LEDGER_ACCOUNT_FK )), 0) + SRC.AMOUNT,
         SRC.NEWBAL_DATE, SRC.LEDGER_ACCOUNT_FK, SRC.COMPANY_FK,
         SRC.REPORTING_TYPE)
   Rationale
      The SQL spent 100% of its database time on CPU, I/O and Cluster waits.
      This part of database time may be improved by the SQL Tuning Advisor.
   Rationale
      Database time for this SQL was divided as follows: 100% for SQL
      execution, 0% for parsing, 0% for PL/SQL execution and 0% for Java
      execution.
   Rationale
      SQL statement with SQL_ID "03rxfh1snby0h" was executed 1 times and had
      an average elapsed time of 848 seconds.
   Rationale
      I/O and Cluster wait for INDEX "PSPADM.PSP_LEDGER_BALANCE_U2" with
      object ID 131148 consumed 48% of the database time spent on this SQL
      statement.
   Rationale
      I/O and Cluster wait for INDEX "PSPADM.SYS_C008675" with object ID
      126855 consumed 47% of the database time spent on this SQL statement.
   Rationale
      Top level calls to execute the PL/SQL statement with SQL_ID
      "3hrt9tdffspr2" are responsible for 100% of the database time spent on
      the UPSERT statement with SQL_ID "03rxfh1snby0h".
      Related Object
         SQL statement with SQL_ID 3hrt9tdffspr2.
         declare
         P_LEDGER_UPDATE_DATE DATE := timestamp '2022-12-07 08:00:00';
         begin
         PSPADM.PRC_CALCULATE_LEDGER_BALANCE(P_LEDGER_UPDATE_DATE =>
         P_LEDGER_UPDATE_DATE);
         end;

   Recommendation 1: Database Configuration
   Estimated benefit is .75 active sessions, 70.07% of total activity.
   -------------------------------------------------------------------

      526592 M.

   ---------------------------------

      Impact is .87 active sessions, 80.82% of total activity.

Finding 1: Undersized SGA
Impact is 1.04 active sessions, 99.98% of total activity.
---------------------------------------------------------
The SGA was inadequately sized, causing additional I/O or hard parses.
The value of parameter "sga_target" was "382976 M" during the analysis period.

   Recommendation 1: Database Configuration
   Estimated benefit is 1.04 active sessions, 99.98% of total activity.
   --------------------------------------------------------------------
   Action
      Increase the size of the SGA by setting the parameter "sga_target" to
      430848 M.

   Symptoms That Led to the Finding:
   ---------------------------------
      Wait class "User I/O" was consuming significant database time.
      Impact is .54 active sessions, 51.84% of total activity.

         FTS.TRANSACTION_STATE_EFF_DATE BETWEEN :B1 - 1 AND :B1 + 1 GROUP BY
         FTS.COMPANY_FK, TRUNC (FTS.TRANSACTION_STATE_EFF_DATE),
         PR.LEDGER_ACCOUNT_FK, PO.REPORTING_TYPE) SRC ON ( TGT.COMPANY_FK =
         SRC.COMPANY_FK AND TGT.REPORTING_TYPE =SRC.REPORTING_TYPE AND

         MODIFIED_DATE = :B2 , VERSION = VERSION+1,

         ILB.COMPANY_FK=SRC.COMPANY_FK AND TRUNC(ILB.BALANCE_DATE) = (SELECT
         TRUNC(MAX(TRUNC(OLB.BALANCE_DATE))) FROM PSP_LEDGER_BALANCE OLB WHERE
         OLB.COMPANY_FK=ILB.COMPANY_FK AND
         OLB.LEDGER_ACCOUNT_FK=ILB.LEDGER_ACCOUNT_FK )), 0) + SRC.AMOUNT,
         SRC.NEWBAL_DATE, SRC.LEDGER_ACCOUNT_FK, SRC.COMPANY_FK,

Impact is .01 active sessions, 1.03% of total activity.
-------------------------------------------------------

analysis period.

   Estimated benefit is .01 active sessions, 1.03% of total activity.

      "pga_aggregate_target" to 30610 M.
